<Time>1539955536941</Time>< Text>
This was my first experience using Snappr. The company is essentially the third party vendor to help match you with a photographer that's right for your event. Whether it's a wedding, personal family shoot, corporate event etc - they will match you with someone in your area and connect you with them. You receive an event link where all your photos will be after the event.
We got connected with Joshua for a business event in Washington DC and he was wonderful to work with. His angels, lighting, candid and posed shots etc were all perfect. My bosses were thrilled to have such great shots documenting their event. I was also very pleased with the fact that our photos were ready within 24 hours and we had full downloading rights to ALL photos.

I currently got an auto loan through Xceed financial. I purchased an F150. My loan processor was Alfredo Reyes from the El Segundo branch in California. I just wanted to thank him and Xceed Financial for the most pleasant loan experience. I had many questions. And he happily answered them all for me. I had contacted him numerous times to make sure I understood the paperwork. He was always available and made sure I understood everything in my contract. When I found the vehicle I wanted to purchase he did a very thorough job making the dealership provide the documentation to make sure I was getting the best deal and was not overpaying for the vehicle. Alfredo and Xceed went above my expectations and provided First Class service that you will not receive from your average bank. Even though the dealership may not have liked all the paperwork he wanted them to send before he approved my loan to ensure the LTV was below 100%. < text>
Small cute restaurant.
Got the greek goddess, which is an egg white omlet, with spinach tomatoes, artachocke, feta and kalamata olives. Has a side of peasent potatoes and an english muffin.
Also got a side of pancakes.
First bite of the omlet was a bit jolting, the kalamata olive was strong. However the rest was very pleasant, good hearty taste and good mixture of ingredients. The potatoes where just a slight variation of country potatoes. They were not over cooked but had a good crunch to them. The pancakes were ok nothing special but also nothing bad. With a little syrup they tasted just like ones from a pancake breakfast.< /text>
